focus_tree = {
	id = russia_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 30
			tag = SOV
		}
	}
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 6300 y = 2200 }
	focus = {
		id = SOV_reign_of_yeltsin
		icon = boris_yeltsin_sheep
		x = 13
		y = 0
		cost = 1
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOV_reign_of_yeltsin"
			add_stability = -0.02
			add_political_power = 50
			country_event = sov_yeltsin.1
			set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
			change_oligarchs_opinion = yes
			set_country_flag = nobody_union_prezik
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { SOV = { is_ai = yes } }
					country_event = { id = russia.61 days = 1 }
				}
				country_event = { id = sov_other.35 days = 100 }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }
	}

	#Start of Putin Branch
	focus = {
		id = SOV_putin
		icon = vladimir_putin
		x = 8
		y = 1
		cost = 2
		available = { emerging_reactionaries_are_in_power = yes }
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_reign_of_yeltsin }
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOV_putin"
			hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SOV_putin_politic_modifier } }
			add_to_variable = { SOV_putin_politic_political_power_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SOV_putin_politic_communism_drift = 0.05 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_putin_politic_start_tt
			set_country_flag = sov_putin_econ
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = sov_putin_econ }
							   clr_country_flag = sov_zug_econ
							   clr_country_flag = sov_zir_econ
					}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } } }
				hidden_effect = {
					clear_array = ruling_party
					clear_array = gov_coalition_array
					add_to_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					update_government_coalition_strength = yes
					update_party_name = yes
					set_coalition_drift = yes
					meta_effect = {
						text = {
							set_country_flag = [META_SET_RULING_PARTY]
						}
						META_SET_RULING_PARTY = "[meta_set_ruling_leader]"
					}
					set_leader = yes
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^6 = 0.075 }
				recalculate_party = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^6 = 0.075 }
				recalculate_party = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.025 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 155
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_PUTIN_PATH
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				has_global_flag = RULE_SUPPORT_KADYR
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 155
				has_global_flag = SOV_OLIGARCHS_RUSSIA_PATH
			}
		}
	}
